The sound of flowing water never ceases, and the song‑like flight of birds gently entices the soul.     translated: "In April, the peach blossoms burst into full bloom, their petals dancing in the gentle breezes and filling the air. Within Peach Blossom Cove, it is serene and secluded. The water is clear with fish swimming, cicadas chirping, birds singing; distant mountains appear like indigo ink, while nearby forests seem like clusters of trees. The sound of flowing water never ceases, and the song‑like flight of birds gently entices the soul. Above Peach Blossom Cove lies a deep cave in the sky, opening suddenly to reveal strange sounds that can be heard as thunderous echoes."

Within the city sat the Flowing Cloud Escort Agency, where noble families, powerful officials, wealthy merchants, and an array of precious and rare treasures gathered in abundance."

Coincidentally, the Saro faction entered the inner regions around this time. Coincidentally, the Saro faction entered the inner regions around this time. The Elder and others from Songshi Mountain accepted the Saro lineage and journeyed far north beyond the passes, establishing Great Snow Mountain where they selected individuals to whom they passed on their teachings."

  - split: 6
    text: "魏、楚、燕三国相互制衡之时，燕国嘉和帝推崇玄门，并且对丹药十分热衷。玉阳真人迟浔江除却剑术的钻研，遍寻炼药之方,为使自身所学得以传承便建立剑斋，将自己的剑法和丹鼎之学尽数相传，待剑斋发展稍稳后便辞去掌门之位，归隐山林。"

Immortal Yu Yang, aside from his research in swordsmanship, tirelessly sought methods for refining elixirs. To ensure that his studies would be passed on, he established Sword Pavilion and imparted both his sword techniques and alchemical knowledge. After the establishment of Sword Pavilion had somewhat stabilized, he resigned from his position as Sect Leader and retreated to live in seclusion among the mountains."

    text: "坐落于楚国腹地，是一座历史悠久的江南名城。淮陵依水而建，四面环水，内有清溪贯穿，外护长江之威，自古便有“水绕淮陵”之美誉。城中古街石巷，楼台倒影于清澈的河水中，烟雨中的淮陵，更是如同一幅水墨画卷，美得令人心醉。"
    translated: "Located in the heartland of the Chu Kingdom, Huailing is an ancient and renowned city in Jiangnan. Built by the water, it is encircled on all sides by rivers, with a clear stream running through its center and protected externally by the majestic Yangtze River. From time immemorial, Huailing has been celebrated for being encircled by water, earning it great acclaim. The city's ancient streets and stone alleys, along with their mirrored reflections of pavilions in the crystal‑clear river waters, make Huailing appear like a scroll painting crafted in ink and wash when shrouded in mist and rain‑an enchanting sight that intoxicates the soul."

  splits:
  - split: 4
    text: "云潇山庄"
    translated: "Cloudy Breeze Mountain Villa"
  - split: 6
    text: "云潇山庄，三面环山，北抵灵川，庄外前者呼，后者应，往来而不绝，庄内山泉汇流，闻水声，如鸣珮环。因靠近江海，遂以商贸作为自身根基，发展商业，逐渐成为楚国第一大家。百年来一直庇佑周围小商户，在江湖上也颇有美名。"
    translated: "Cloudy Breeze Mountain Villa is surrounded by mountains on three sides and borders Lingchuan to the north. Those who pass by outside call out and receive responses, ensuring a constant flow of visitors coming and going. Within the villa, mountain streams converge, producing a water sound resembling that of tinkling jade pendants. Due to its proximity to the river and sea, it established commerce as its foundation, developing trade and gradually becoming the largest family in the Chu Kingdom.   splits:
  - split: 4
    text: "仙洲"
    translated: "Immortal Isle"
  - split: 6
    text: "仙洲，相传为海外无底之谷，玄门仙师乘舟历经数年得见其形，因其汇聚天下之水而无增无减，称为归墟。居岛中数年，体悟天地大道，得窥玄门之愿有道无相，遂将毕生感悟刻与石碑之上，以待有缘之人。"
    translated: "Immortal Isle, fabled to be an endless abyss beyond the sea, was glimpsed by a Xuanmen Immortal Master who sailed for several years. Because it gathers all of the world's waters yet never increases or decreases in volume, it is called the Return Haven. After dwelling on the island for several years and understanding the great Way of Heaven and Earth, he realized his wish to glimpse the essence of Xuanmen‑having a path without form‑and inscribed his life‑long insights on stone tablets, waiting for someone with destiny to discover them."

    text: "绝世隐秘之所，隐藏在云雾缭绕的高山之巅，修炼的绝佳之所，也是许多珍稀药材和武林秘籍的出产地。有些福地盛产能助人突破瓶颈的仙草奇花，有些则藏有能增强内功、提升武艺的秘籍和宝物。因此，七十二福地成为了武林中众多门派、江湖侠客争相寻找的宝地。"

It is an ideal location for cultivation and the source of many rare medicinal herbs and martial world secret texts. Some blessings lands produce exceptional plants that aid practitioners in breaking through plateaus, while others contain treasures and texts that enhance neigong and improve martial arts skills. Consequently, the Seventy‑Two Blessings Lands have become a sought‑after treasure trove for numerous martial world sects and Jianghu wanderers."

Consequently, many astonishing swords lie within this sword mound."

Consequently, many astonishing swords lie within this sword mound."

    text: "涧水清冽，绕岩穿林声绵延，苍松翠竹，护此一隅天地宁；步石渡流，轻烟浅唱鹿鸣初，寻幽访胜，心灵洗涤尘世除。崇吾涧下，时见行者凭栏歌，此涧不仅山清水秀景色佳，更有灵气，吸引修者来打坐，洞悉天地至理。"

Stones serve as stepping paths across the flow while faint mist rises with the initial call of deer. Exploring hidden spots for their charm refreshes the spirit, purging worldly concerns. Below Chongwu Valley, one often sees travelers leaning on railings to sing. This valley is not only known for its stunning scenery and picturesque views but also for a mysterious energy that attracts practitioners to meditate here, gaining insight into the ultimate truths of heaven and earth."

Although it cannot be compared to the most illustrious sects in Jianghu, its members are known for their integrity and honor, earning considerable respect within Jianghu."

The seasons are distinct: peach blossoms reflect on spring waters; summer is filled with cicadas' songs; autumn yields bountiful harvests while winter brings snow. This place remains untouched by worldly dust, free from fame and profit, embodying a simple way of life where time passes peacefully.   - split: 6
    text: "荒凉戈壁，辽阔无际。凄迷寸草，唯见孤丘点缀。风悠然，沙漫漫，似千军万马，奔涌汹涌，黄埃扑面，令人心胆俱寒。无人迹，寂无声。独鹰徘徊，孤星若点。骆驼嘶鸣，搜寻几缕韧草，艰难度日。深藏宝物，引得豪杰往来。"
    translated: "The barren Gobi stretches out limitlessly. In this desolate expanse, not a blade of grass can be seen; only solitary hills dot the landscape. The wind blows gently across endless dunes, as if thousands of troops and horses charge in an overwhelming surge, with yellow dust enveloping everything, chilling one to the bone. It is devoid of human presence and silent beyond measure. A lone eagle hovers overhead while a solitary star glimmers in the sky. Camels call out, searching for sparse tufts of resilient grass to sustain themselves through tough days. Hidden treasures lie beneath the surface, attracting heroes from afar"
